TEST 01 | customer_sets | hard | Gold customers with delivered online activity
========================================================================================================================
HTTP STATUS: 200
ENDPOINT SUCCESS: True
ELAPSED SECONDS: 95.38

NATURAL-LANGUAGE QUERIES
Q1: Which active Gold customers placed a delivered online order in 2025?
Q2: Which Gold customers placed a delivered order in 2025?
Q3: Which active customers placed an online order in 2025?
Q4: Which customers had a failed payment and no delivered orders?

EXPECTED LOGICAL RELATIONSHIPS
- Q1 is contained in Q2.
- Q1 is contained in Q3.
- Q4 is not implied by Q1, Q2, or Q3.

GENERATED SQL
Q2: success=True safe=True rows=10 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=100.0
SELECT DISTINCT c.customer_id, c.first_name, c.last_name
FROM customers c
JOIN sales_orders so ON c.customer_id = so.customer_id
WHERE c.loyalty_tier = 'gold'
  AND c.account_status = 'active'
  AND so.order_status = 'delivered'
  AND so.sales_channel = 'online'
  AND so.order_date LIKE '2025%'
Q3: success=True safe=True rows=34 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=100.0
SELECT c.customer_id, c.first_name, c.last_name
FROM customers c
JOIN sales_orders o ON c.customer_id = o.customer_id
WHERE c.loyalty_tier = 'gold'
  AND o.order_status = 'delivered'
  AND o.order_date LIKE '2025%'
GROUP BY c.customer_id
HAVING COUNT(o.order_id) > 0
Q4: success=True safe=True rows=64 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=100.0
SELECT c.customer_id, c.first_name, c.last_name
FROM customers c
JOIN sales_orders so ON c.customer_id = so.customer_id
WHERE c.account_status = 'active'
  AND so.sales_channel = 'online'
  AND so.order_date LIKE '2025%'
GROUP BY c.customer_id, c.first_name, c.last_name
Q5: success=True safe=True rows=17 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=100.0
SELECT c.customer_id, c.first_name, c.last_name
FROM customers c
JOIN payments p ON c.customer_id = p.customer_id
JOIN sales_orders so ON p.order_id = so.order_id
JOIN shipments sh ON so.order_id = sh.order_id
WHERE p.payment_status = 'failed'
  AND NOT EXISTS (
    SELECT 1
    FROM shipments sh2
    JOIN sales_orders so2 ON sh2.order_id = so2.order_id
    WHERE so2.customer_id = c.customer_id
      AND sh2.shipment_status = 'delivered'
  )
GROUP BY c.customer_id, c.first_name, c.last_name

========================================================================================================================
TEST 02 | customer_sets | hard | Enterprise customers and settled card payments
========================================================================================================================
HTTP STATUS: 200
ENDPOINT SUCCESS: True
ELAPSED SECONDS: 80.27

NATURAL-LANGUAGE QUERIES
Q1: Which enterprise customers have made a settled credit-card payment?
Q2: Which customers have made at least one settled payment?
Q3: Which enterprise customers have ever paid by credit card?
Q4: Which customers have payments but have never had one settle successfully?

EXPECTED LOGICAL RELATIONSHIPS
- Q1 is contained in Q2.
- Q1 is contained in Q3.
- Q4 is a different customer set.

GENERATED SQL
Q2: success=True safe=True rows=12 source=llm_primary score=100.0
SELECT DISTINCT "customers"."customer_id", "customers"."customer_number", "customers"."full_name" FROM "customers" INNER JOIN "payments" ON "customers"."customer_id" = "payments"."customer_id" WHERE "customers"."customer_segment" = ? AND "payments"."payment_method" = ? AND "payments"."payment_status" = ?
Q3: success=True safe=True rows=257 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=100.0
SELECT c.customer_id, c.first_name, c.last_name
FROM customers c
JOIN payments p ON c.customer_id = p.customer_id
GROUP BY c.customer_id
HAVING COUNT(CASE WHEN p.payment_status = 'settled' THEN 1 END) > 0
Q4: success=True safe=True rows=15 source=llm_sql_repair score=93.0
SELECT "customers"."customer_id", "customers"."full_name"
FROM "customers"
INNER JOIN "payments" ON "customers"."customer_id" = "payments"."customer_id"
WHERE "customers"."customer_segment" = 'enterprise'
  AND "payments"."payment_method" = 'credit_card'
GROUP BY "customers"."customer_id", "customers"."full_name"

Q2: success=True safe=True rows=36 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=100.0
SELECT DISTINCT c.customer_id, c.first_name, c.last_name
FROM customers c
JOIN sales_orders so ON c.customer_id = so.customer_id
JOIN addresses a ON so.shipping_address_id = a.address_id
WHERE c.account_status = 'active'
  AND so.order_status = 'delivered'
  AND a.residential_flag = '1'
  AND a.state_code = 'WA'
Q3: success=True safe=True rows=50 source=llm_sql_direct_grain score=76.0
SELECT c.customer_id, c.first_name, c.last_name
FROM customers c
JOIN sales_orders so ON c.customer_id = so.customer_id
JOIN shipments s ON so.order_id = s.order_id
JOIN addresses a ON s.shipping_address_id = a.address_id
WHERE s.shipment_status = 'delivered'
  AND a.state_code = 'WA'
GROUP BY c.customer_id, c.first_name, c.last_name
Q4: success=True safe=True rows=211 source=llm_sql_direct_grain score=100.0
SELECT c.customer_id, c.first_name, c.last_name
FROM customers c
JOIN addresses a ON c.customer_id = a.customer_id
JOIN sales_orders o ON c.customer_id = o.customer_id
WHERE c.account_status = 'active'
  AND a.residential_flag = '1'
  AND a.address_type IN ('shipping', 'both')
GROUP BY c.customer_id, c.first_name, c.last_name
Q5: success=True safe=True rows=135 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=87.0
SELECT c.customer_id, c.first_name, c.last_name
FROM customers c
JOIN sales_orders so ON c.customer_id = so.customer_id
JOIN addresses ba ON so.billing_address_id = ba.address_id
JOIN addresses sa ON so.shipping_address_id = sa.address_id
WHERE ba.state_code != sa.state_code
GROUP BY c.customer_id, c.first_name, c.last_name

========================================================================================================================
TEST 04 | customer_sets | hard | Customers across product categories
========================================================================================================================
HTTP STATUS: 200
ENDPOINT SUCCESS: True
ELAPSED SECONDS: 110.79

NATURAL-LANGUAGE QUERIES
Q1: Which customers bought both Electronics and Outdoors products but never bought Apparel?
Q2: Which customers have bought an Electronics product?
Q3: Which customers have bought an Outdoors product?
Q4: Which customers bought Apparel but have never bought Electronics?

EXPECTED LOGICAL RELATIONSHIPS
- Q1 is contained in Q2.
- Q1 is contained in Q3.
- Q1 and Q4 should be disjoint.

GENERATED SQL
Q2: success=True safe=True rows=42 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=85.0
SELECT c.customer_id, c.first_name, c.last_name
FROM customers c
JOIN sales_orders so ON c.customer_id = so.customer_id
JOIN sales_order_items soi ON so.order_id = soi.order_id
JOIN products p ON soi.product_id = p.product_id
GROUP BY c.customer_id, c.first_name, c.last_name
HAVING COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN p.category = 'Electronics' THEN p.category END) > 0
   AND COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN p.category = 'Outdoors' THEN p.category END) > 0
   AND COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN p.category = 'Apparel' THEN p.category END) = 0
Q3: success=True safe=True rows=203 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=79.0
SELECT c.customer_id, c.first_name, c.last_name
FROM customers c
JOIN sales_orders so ON c.customer_id = so.customer_id
JOIN sales_order_items soi ON so.order_id = soi.order_id
JOIN products p ON soi.product_id = p.product_id
WHERE p.category = 'Electronics'
GROUP BY c.customer_id, c.first_name, c.last_name
Q4: success=True safe=True rows=169 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=79.0
SELECT c.customer_id, c.first_name, c.last_name
FROM customers c
JOIN sales_orders so ON c.customer_id = so.customer_id
JOIN sales_order_items soi ON so.order_id = soi.order_id
JOIN products p ON soi.product_id = p.product_id
WHERE p.category = 'Outdoors'
GROUP BY c.customer_id, c.first_name, c.last_name
Q5: success=True safe=True rows=30 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=99.0
SELECT c.customer_id, c.first_name, c.last_name
FROM customers c
JOIN sales_orders so ON c.customer_id = so.customer_id
JOIN sales_order_items soi ON so.order_id = soi.order_id
JOIN products p ON soi.product_id = p.product_id
WHERE p.category = 'Apparel'
  AND NOT EXISTS (
    SELECT 1
    FROM sales_order_items soi2
    JOIN products p2 ON soi2.product_id = p2.product_id
    WHERE soi2.order_id IN (
      SELECT order_id
      FROM sales_orders
      WHERE customer_id = c.customer_id
    )
    AND p2.category = 'Electronics'
  )
GROUP BY c.customer_id, c.first_name, c.last_name

========================================================================================================================
TEST 05 | customer_sets | hard | Refunded Gold-customer orders
========================================================================================================================
HTTP STATUS: 200
ENDPOINT SUCCESS: True
ELAPSED SECONDS: 77.63

NATURAL-LANGUAGE QUERIES
Q1: Which Gold customers received a refund on an order that was eventually delivered?
Q2: Which customers have received any refund?
Q3: Which Gold customers have had a delivered order?
Q4: Which customers have settled payments but no refunded payments?

EXPECTED LOGICAL RELATIONSHIPS
- Q1 is contained in Q2.
- Q1 is contained in Q3.
- Q4 is not a superset of Q1.

GENERATED SQL
Q2: success=True safe=True rows=0 source=llm_sql_repair score=100.0
SELECT c.customer_id, c.first_name, c.last_name
FROM customers c
JOIN payments p ON c.customer_id = p.customer_id
JOIN sales_orders o ON p.order_id = o.order_id
WHERE c.loyalty_tier = 'gold'
  AND p.payment_status = 'refunded'
  AND o.fulfillment_status = 'fulfilled'
GROUP BY c.customer_id, c.first_name, c.last_name
Q3: success=True safe=True rows=32 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=95.0
SELECT c.customer_id, c.first_name, c.last_name
FROM customers c
JOIN payments p ON c.customer_id = p.customer_id
GROUP BY c.customer_id, c.first_name, c.last_name
HAVING SUM(p.refunded_amount) > 0
Q4: success=True safe=True rows=58 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=100.0
SELECT c.customer_id, c.first_name, c.last_name
FROM customers c
JOIN sales_orders so ON c.customer_id = so.customer_id
WHERE c.loyalty_tier = 'gold'
GROUP BY c.customer_id
HAVING COUNT(CASE WHEN so.order_status = 'delivered' THEN 1 END) > 0
Q5: success=True safe=True rows=225 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=100.0
SELECT c.customer_id, c.first_name, c.last_name
FROM customers c
JOIN payments p ON c.customer_id = p.customer_id
WHERE p.payment_status = 'settled'
  AND NOT EXISTS (
    SELECT 1
    FROM payments p2
    WHERE p2.customer_id = c.customer_id
      AND p2.refunded_amount > 0
  )
GROUP BY c.customer_id, c.first_name, c.last_name

========================================================================================================================
TEST 09 | sales_order_sets | hard | Settled card payments with refunds
========================================================================================================================
HTTP STATUS: 200
ENDPOINT SUCCESS: True
ELAPSED SECONDS: 73.36

NATURAL-LANGUAGE QUERIES
Q1: Which orders have a settled credit-card payment with a positive refunded amount?
Q2: Which orders have at least one settled payment?
Q3: Which orders have a credit-card payment that was partly or fully refunded?
Q4: Which orders have failed payments and no successful payment?

EXPECTED LOGICAL RELATIONSHIPS
- Q1 is contained in Q2.
- Q1 is contained in Q3.
- Q4 is a different order set.

GENERATED SQL
Q2: success=True safe=True rows=7 source=llm_primary score=98.0
SELECT DISTINCT "sales_orders"."order_id" FROM "sales_orders" INNER JOIN "payments" ON "sales_orders"."order_id" = "payments"."order_id" WHERE "payments"."payment_method" = ? AND "payments"."payment_status" = ? AND "payments"."refunded_amount" > ?
Q3: success=True safe=True rows=609 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=75.0
SELECT so.order_id, so.order_number
FROM sales_orders so
WHERE EXISTS (
    SELECT 1
    FROM payments p
    WHERE p.order_id = so.order_id
      AND p.payment_status = 'settled'
)
Q4: success=True safe=True rows=7 source=llm_primary score=91.0
SELECT DISTINCT "sales_orders"."order_id" FROM "sales_orders" INNER JOIN "payments" ON "sales_orders"."order_id" = "payments"."order_id" WHERE "payments"."payment_method" = ? AND "payments"."refunded_amount" > ?
Q5: success=True safe=True rows=105 source=llm_sql_repair score=100.0
SELECT so.order_id, so.order_number
FROM sales_orders so
WHERE EXISTS (
    SELECT 1
    FROM payments p
    WHERE p.order_id = so.order_id
    AND p.payment_status = 'failed'
)
AND NOT EXISTS (
    SELECT 1
    FROM payments p2
    WHERE p2.order_id = so.order_id
    AND p2.payment_status IN ('authorized', 'settled')
)

NATURAL-LANGUAGE QUERIES
Q1: Which orders were shipped from a temperature-controlled Northwest warehouse to a residential address in Washington?
Q2: Which orders were shipped from a temperature-controlled warehouse?
Q3: Which orders were sent to a residential address in Washington?
Q4: Which orders have never been shipped?

EXPECTED LOGICAL RELATIONSHIPS
- Q1 is contained in Q2.
- Q1 is contained in Q3.
- Q4 should be disjoint from Q1.

GENERATED SQL
Q2: success=True safe=True rows=0 source=llm_sql_repair score=95.0
SELECT DISTINCT so.order_id, so.order_number
FROM sales_orders so
JOIN shipments s ON so.order_id = s.order_id
JOIN warehouses w ON s.warehouse_id = w.warehouse_id
JOIN addresses a ON s.shipping_address_id = a.address_id
WHERE w.temperature_controlled = 1
  AND w.region = 'Northwest'
  AND w.state_code = 'WA'
  AND a.residential_flag = 1
  AND a.state_code = 'WA'
Q3: success=True safe=True rows=321 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=89.0

JOIN warehouses w ON s.warehouse_id = w.warehouse_id
WHERE w.temperature_controlled = 1
Q4: success=True safe=True rows=97 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=95.0
SELECT so.order_id, so.order_number
FROM sales_orders so
JOIN addresses a ON so.shipping_address_id = a.address_id
WHERE a.state_code = 'WA' AND a.residential_flag = '1'
Q5: success=True safe=True rows=0 source=llm_sql_repair score=96.0
SELECT so.order_id, so.order_number
FROM sales_orders so
LEFT JOIN shipments s ON so.order_id = s.order_id
WHERE s.shipment_id IS NULL

Q2: Which discontinued products still have available inventory?

EXPECTED LOGICAL RELATIONSHIPS

- Q1 is contained in Q3.

GENERATED SQL
Q2: success=True safe=True rows=7 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=95.0
SELECT p.product_id, p.product_name, p.sku
FROM products p
JOIN inventory i ON p.product_id = i.product_id
JOIN sales_order_items soi ON p.product_id = soi.product_id
WHERE p.discontinued_flag = 1
  AND i.quantity_available > 0
  AND soi.order_id IN (
    SELECT order_id
    FROM sales_orders
    WHERE order_date LIKE '2025-%'
  )
GROUP BY p.product_id
Q3: success=True safe=True rows=34 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=93.0
SELECT p.product_id, p.product_name, p.sku
FROM products p
JOIN inventory i ON p.product_id = i.product_id
WHERE p.discontinued_flag = 1
  AND i.quantity_available > 0
Q4: success=True safe=True rows=53 source=llm_sql_repair score=93.0
SELECT p.product_id, p.product_name
FROM products p
JOIN sales_order_items soi ON p.product_id = soi.product_id
GROUP BY p.product_id, p.product_name
HAVING strftime('%Y', soi.created_at) = '2025'
Q5: success=True safe=True rows=0 source=llm_sql_repair score=99.0
SELECT p.product_id, p.product_name
FROM products p
WHERE NOT EXISTS (
    SELECT 1
    FROM sales_order_items soi
    WHERE soi.product_id = p.product_id
)

    FROM inventory i

========================================================================================================================
TEST 13 | product_sets | hard | Products sold across channels
========================================================================================================================
HTTP STATUS: 200
ENDPOINT SUCCESS: True
ELAPSED SECONDS: 79.43

NATURAL-LANGUAGE QUERIES
Q1: Which products were sold through both online and store orders but never through partner orders?
Q2: Which products were sold through online orders?
Q3: Which products were sold through store orders?
Q4: Which products were sold through partner orders but never online?

EXPECTED LOGICAL RELATIONSHIPS
- Q1 is contained in Q2.
- Q1 is contained in Q3.
- Q1 and Q4 should be disjoint.

GENERATED SQL
Q2: success=True safe=True rows=84 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=100.0
SELECT p.product_id, p.product_name
FROM products p
JOIN sales_order_items soi ON p.product_id = soi.product_id
JOIN sales_orders so ON soi.order_id = so.order_id
GROUP BY p.product_id, p.product_name
HAVING COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN so.sales_channel = 'online' THEN 1 END) > 0
   AND COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN so.sales_channel = 'store' THEN 1 END) > 0
   AND NOT EXISTS (
       SELECT 1
       FROM sales_order_items soi2
       JOIN sales_orders so2 ON soi2.order_id = so2.order_id
       WHERE soi2.product_id = p.product_id
         AND so2.sales_channel = 'partner'
   )
Q3: success=True safe=True rows=390 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=95.0
SELECT DISTINCT p.product_id, p.product_name
FROM products p
JOIN sales_order_items soi ON p.product_id = soi.product_id
JOIN sales_orders so ON soi.order_id = so.order_id
WHERE so.sales_channel = 'online'
Q4: success=True safe=True rows=376 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=75.0
SELECT DISTINCT p.product_id, p.product_name
FROM products p
JOIN sales_order_items soi ON p.product_id = soi.product_id
JOIN sales_orders so ON soi.order_id = so.order_id
WHERE so.sales_channel = 'store'
Q5: success=True safe=True rows=109 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=98.0
SELECT p.product_id, p.product_name
FROM products p
JOIN sales_order_items soi ON p.product_id = soi.product_id
JOIN sales_orders so ON soi.order_id = so.order_id
GROUP BY p.product_id, p.product_name
HAVING COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN so.sales_channel != 'online' THEN so.order_id END) > 0
   AND NOT EXISTS (
       SELECT 1
       FROM sales_order_items soi2
       JOIN sales_orders so2 ON soi2.order_id = so2.order_id
       WHERE soi2.product_id = p.product_id
         AND so2.sales_channel = 'online'
   )

TEST 14 | product_sets | hard | Ordered products with inadequate stock
========================================================================================================================
HTTP STATUS: 200
ENDPOINT SUCCESS: True
ELAPSED SECONDS: 73.47

NATURAL-LANGUAGE QUERIES
Q1: Which low-stock products have total ordered quantity greater than their current available inventory?
Q2: Which products have been ordered in a quantity greater than their available inventory?
Q3: Which products are currently low in stock?
Q4: Which products have never appeared on an order?

EXPECTED LOGICAL RELATIONSHIPS
- Q1 is contained in Q2.
- Q1 is contained in Q3.
- Q4 should not contain Q1.

GENERATED SQL
Q2: success=True safe=True rows=234 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=90.0
SELECT p.product_id, p.product_name, i.quantity_available
FROM products p
JOIN inventory i ON p.product_id = i.product_id
JOIN sales_order_items soi ON p.product_id = soi.product_id
GROUP BY p.product_id, p.product_name, i.quantity_available
HAVING SUM(soi.quantity_ordered) > i.quantity_available
WARNINGS: ['selected SQL: possible join fanout aggregate inflation']
Q3: success=True safe=True rows=234 source=llm_variant score=90.0
SELECT "inventory"."quantity_available", "products"."product_id", "products"."product_name", SUM("sales_order_items"."quantity_ordered") AS "total_ordered" FROM "products" INNER JOIN "inventory" ON "products"."product_id" = "inventory"."product_id" INNER JOIN "sales_order_items" ON "products"."product_id" = "sales_order_items"."product_id" GROUP BY "products"."product_id", "products"."product_name", "inventory"."quantity_available" HAVING "total_ordered" > "quantity_available"
WARNINGS: ['selected SQL: possible join fanout aggregate inflation']
Q4: success=True safe=True rows=155 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=100.0
SELECT p.product_id, p.product_name, i.quantity_on_hand
FROM products p
JOIN inventory i ON p.product_id = i.product_id
WHERE i.quantity_on_hand < i.reorder_point
Q5: success=True safe=True rows=1 source=llm_sql_direct score=99.0
SELECT p.product_id, p.product_name
FROM products p
WHERE NOT EXISTS (
    SELECT 1
    FROM sales_order_items soi
    WHERE soi.product_id = p.product_id
)

========================================================================================================================
TEST 15 | product_sets | hard | Products above category benchmarks
========================================================================================================================
HTTP STATUS: 200
ENDPOINT SUCCESS: True
ELAPSED SECONDS: 99.61

NATURAL-LANGUAGE QUERIES
Q1: Which products are priced above their category average and also have a gross margin above their category average?
Q2: Which products are priced above the average sale price for their category?
Q3: Which products have a gross margin percentage above their category average?
Q4: Which products are priced below the overall average sale price?

EXPECTED LOGICAL RELATIONSHIPS
- Q1 is contained in Q2.
- Q1 is contained in Q3.
- Q4 is not implied by the first three.

GENERATED SQL
Q2: success=True safe=True rows=203 source=llm_sql_direct_grain score=100.0
SELECT p.product_id, p.product_name, p.list_price, p.standard_cost
FROM products p
WHERE p.list_price > (
    SELECT AVG(p2.list_price)
    FROM products p2
    WHERE p2.category = p.category
)
AND (p.list_price - p.standard_cost) > (
    SELECT AVG(p2.list_price - p2.standard_cost)
    FROM products p2
    WHERE p2.category = p.category
)
Q3: success=True safe=True rows=243 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=100.0
SELECT p.product_id, p.product_name, p.category, p.sale_price
FROM products p
WHERE p.sale_price > (
    SELECT AVG(p2.sale_price)
    FROM products p2
    WHERE p2.category = p.category
)
Q4: success=True safe=True rows=282 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=100.0
SELECT p.product_id, p.product_name, p.category, p.standard_cost, p.sale_price
FROM products p
WHERE p.standard_cost IS NOT NULL AND p.standard_cost > 0
  AND (1.0 - p.standard_cost / p.sale_price) > (
    SELECT AVG(1.0 - p2.standard_cost / p2.sale_price)
    FROM products p2
    WHERE p2.category = p.category
      AND p2.standard_cost IS NOT NULL
      AND p2.standard_cost > 0
  )
Q5: success=True safe=True rows=256 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=99.0
SELECT products.product_id, products.product_name, products.sale_price
FROM products
WHERE products.sale_price < (SELECT AVG(sale_price) FROM products)

========================================================================================================================
TEST 16 | supplier_sets | hard | High-risk suppliers with active sales
========================================================================================================================
HTTP STATUS: 200
ENDPOINT SUCCESS: True
ELAPSED SECONDS: 88.67

NATURAL-LANGUAGE QUERIES
Q1: Which active high-risk suppliers have low-stock products that appeared on delivered orders?
Q2: Which high-risk suppliers provide at least one low-stock product?
Q3: Which active suppliers had a product appear on a delivered order?
Q4: Which inactive suppliers have no products on any order?

EXPECTED LOGICAL RELATIONSHIPS
- Q1 is contained in Q2.
- Q1 is contained in Q3.
- Q4 is a different supplier set.

GENERATED SQL
Q2: success=True safe=True rows=5 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=93.0
SELECT s.supplier_id, s.supplier_name, s.risk_level
FROM suppliers s
JOIN products p ON s.supplier_id = p.supplier_id
JOIN inventory i ON p.product_id = i.product_id
JOIN sales_order_items soi ON p.product_id = soi.product_id
JOIN sales_orders so ON soi.order_id = so.order_id
WHERE s.risk_level = 'high'
  AND i.quantity_on_hand < i.reorder_point
  AND so.order_status = 'delivered'
GROUP BY s.supplier_id, s.supplier_name, s.risk_level
HAVING COUNT(DISTINCT p.product_id) > 0
Q3: success=True safe=True rows=5 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=84.0
SELECT s.supplier_id, s.supplier_name
FROM suppliers s
JOIN products p ON s.supplier_id = p.supplier_id
JOIN inventory i ON p.product_id = i.product_id
WHERE s.risk_level = 'high'
  AND i.quantity_on_hand <= i.reorder_point
GROUP BY s.supplier_id, s.supplier_name
Q4: success=True safe=True rows=55 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=86.0
SELECT s.supplier_id, s.supplier_name
FROM suppliers s
JOIN products p ON s.supplier_id = p.supplier_id
JOIN sales_order_items soi ON p.product_id = soi.product_id
JOIN shipments sh ON soi.order_id = sh.order_id
WHERE s.active_flag = '1'
  AND sh.shipment_status = 'delivered'
GROUP BY s.supplier_id, s.supplier_name
Q5: success=True safe=True rows=0 source=llm_sql_repair score=88.0
SELECT s.supplier_id, s.supplier_name
FROM suppliers s
WHERE s.active_flag = '0'
AND NOT EXISTS (
    SELECT 1
    FROM products p
    JOIN sales_order_items soi ON p.product_id = soi.product_id
    WHERE p.supplier_id = s.supplier_id
)

Q4: Which suppliers have products with no inventory records?

Q2: success=True safe=True rows=60 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=100.0
SELECT s.supplier_id, s.supplier_name
FROM suppliers s
JOIN products p ON s.supplier_id = p.supplier_id
JOIN inventory i ON p.product_id = i.product_id
JOIN sales_order_items soi ON p.product_id = soi.product_id
JOIN sales_orders so ON soi.order_id = so.order_id
JOIN customers c ON so.customer_id = c.customer_id
WHERE c.loyalty_tier = 'gold'
GROUP BY s.supplier_id, s.supplier_name
HAVING COUNT(DISTINCT i.warehouse_id) >= 3

========================================================================================================================
TEST 18 | supplier_sets | hard | Suppliers spanning product categories
========================================================================================================================
HTTP STATUS: 200
ENDPOINT SUCCESS: True
ELAPSED SECONDS: 83.12

NATURAL-LANGUAGE QUERIES
Q1: Which suppliers provide both Electronics and Apparel products but no Automotive products?
Q2: Which suppliers provide Electronics products?
Q3: Which suppliers provide Apparel products?
Q4: Which suppliers provide Automotive products and no Electronics products?

EXPECTED LOGICAL RELATIONSHIPS
- Q1 is contained in Q2.
- Q1 is contained in Q3.
- Q1 and Q4 should be disjoint.

GENERATED SQL
Q2: success=True safe=True rows=11 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=100.0
SELECT s.supplier_id, s.supplier_name
FROM suppliers s
JOIN products p ON s.supplier_id = p.supplier_id
GROUP BY s.supplier_id, s.supplier_name
HAVING COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN p.category = 'Electronics' THEN p.product_id END) > 0
   AND COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN p.category = 'Apparel' THEN p.product_id END) > 0
   AND COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN p.category = 'Automotive' THEN p.product_id END) = 0
Q3: success=True safe=True rows=42 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=93.0
SELECT DISTINCT s.supplier_id, s.supplier_name
FROM suppliers s
JOIN products p ON s.supplier_id = p.supplier_id
WHERE p.category = 'Electronics'
Q4: success=True safe=True rows=34 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=93.0
SELECT DISTINCT s.supplier_id, s.supplier_name
FROM suppliers s
JOIN products p ON s.supplier_id = p.supplier_id
WHERE p.category = 'Apparel'
Q5: success=True safe=True rows=12 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=100.0
SELECT s.supplier_id, s.supplier_name
FROM suppliers s
JOIN products p ON s.supplier_id = p.supplier_id
WHERE s.supplier_id IN (
    SELECT supplier_id
    FROM products
    WHERE category = 'Automotive'
)
AND s.supplier_id NOT IN (
    SELECT supplier_id
    FROM products
    WHERE category = 'Electronics'
)
GROUP BY s.supplier_id, s.supplier_name

CONTAINMENT SUMMARY
None: status=narrower_query | contained_in=[2, 3] | contains=- | equivalent_to=- | incomparable_with=[4] | unknown_with=-

Q4: success=True safe=True rows=60 source=llm_sql_repair score=100.0

FROM suppliers s

GROUP BY s.supplier_id, s.supplier_name

Q5: success=True safe=True rows=0 source=llm_primary score=77.0

AND "suppliers"."active_flag" = ? AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM "products" WHERE "suppliers"."supplier_id" = "products"."supplier_id" AND "products"."list_price" > ?) NATURAL-LANGUAGE QUERIES
Q1: Which suppliers have above-average product revenue and an average product sale price above the overall product average?
Q2: Which suppliers have product revenue above the average supplier revenue?
Q3: Which suppliers have an average product sale price above the overall product average?
Q4: Which suppliers have products that have never been ordered?

EXPECTED LOGICAL RELATIONSHIPS
- Q1 is contained in Q2.
- Q1 is contained in Q3.
- Q4 is not implied by the first three.

GENERATED SQL
Q2: success=True safe=True rows=23 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=99.0
SELECT s.supplier_id, s.supplier_name
FROM suppliers s
JOIN products p ON s.supplier_id = p.supplier_id
JOIN sales_order_items soi ON p.product_id = soi.product_id
GROUP BY s.supplier_id, s.supplier_name
HAVING AVG(soi.line_total) > (SELECT AVG(line_total) FROM sales_order_items)
   AND AVG(soi.unit_price) > (SELECT AVG(unit_price) FROM sales_order_items)
Q3: success=True safe=True rows=22 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=89.0
SELECT s.supplier_id, s.supplier_name
FROM suppliers s
JOIN products p ON s.supplier_id = p.supplier_id
JOIN sales_order_items soi ON p.product_id = soi.product_id
GROUP BY s.supplier_id, s.supplier_name
HAVING SUM(soi.line_total) > (
    SELECT AVG(supplier_total)
    FROM (
        SELECT SUM(soi2.line_total) AS supplier_total
        FROM products p2
        JOIN sales_order_items soi2 ON p2.product_id = soi2.product_id
        GROUP BY p2.supplier_id
    )
)
WARNINGS: ['selected SQL: possible join fanout aggregate inflation']
Q4: success=True safe=True rows=31 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=100.0
SELECT s.supplier_id, s.supplier_name
FROM suppliers s
JOIN products p ON s.supplier_id = p.supplier_id
GROUP BY s.supplier_id, s.supplier_name
HAVING AVG(p.sale_price) > (SELECT AVG(sale_price) FROM products)
Q5: success=True safe=True rows=0 source=llm_sql_repair score=87.0
SELECT s.supplier_id, s.supplier_name
FROM suppliers s
WHERE NOT EXISTS (
    SELECT 1
    FROM products p
    JOIN sales_order_items soi ON p.product_id = soi.product_id
    WHERE p.supplier_id = s.supplier_id
)

GENERATED SQL
Q2: success=True safe=True rows=6 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=100.0
SELECT e.employee_id, e.first_name, e.last_name, e.salary, d.department_name
FROM employees e
JOIN departments d ON e.department_id = d.department_id
WHERE e.employment_status = 'active'
  AND e.employment_type = 'full-time'
  AND e.salary > 100000
  AND d.compliance_level = 'high'

========================================================================================================================
TEST 22 | employee_sets | hard | Warehouse managers who also sell
========================================================================================================================
HTTP STATUS: 200
ENDPOINT SUCCESS: True
ELAPSED SECONDS: 79.90

NATURAL-LANGUAGE QUERIES
Q1: Which employees both manage a warehouse and have handled at least one sales order?
Q2: Which employees manage a warehouse?
Q3: Which employees have handled a sales order?
Q4: Which employees neither manage a warehouse nor appear as a sales representative?

EXPECTED LOGICAL RELATIONSHIPS
- Q1 is contained in Q2.
- Q1 is contained in Q3.
- Q4 should be disjoint from Q1.

GENERATED SQL
Q2: success=True safe=True rows=0 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=91.0
SELECT e.employee_id, e.first_name, e.last_name
FROM employees e
JOIN warehouses w ON e.employee_id = w.manager_employee_id
JOIN sales_orders so ON e.employee_id = so.sales_rep_id
GROUP BY e.employee_id
HAVING COUNT(DISTINCT w.warehouse_id) > 0
   AND COUNT(DISTINCT so.order_id) > 0
Q3: success=True safe=True rows=12 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=91.0
SELECT e.employee_id, e.first_name, e.last_name
FROM employees e
JOIN warehouses w ON e.employee_id = w.manager_employee_id
Q4: success=True safe=True rows=20 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=91.0
SELECT e.employee_id, e.first_name, e.last_name
FROM employees e
JOIN sales_orders so ON e.employee_id = so.sales_rep_id
GROUP BY e.employee_id
Q5: success=True safe=True rows=93 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=94.0
SELECT e.employee_id, e.first_name, e.last_name
FROM employees e
WHERE NOT EXISTS (
    SELECT 1
    FROM warehouses w
    WHERE w.manager_employee_id = e.employee_id
)
AND NOT EXISTS (
    SELECT 1
    FROM sales_orders so
    WHERE so.sales_rep_id = e.employee_id
)

FROM employees e
JOIN sales_orders so ON e.employee_id = so.sales_rep_id
JOIN customers c ON so.customer_id = c.customer_id

SELECT e.employee_id, e.first_name, e.last_name
FROM employees e
WHERE EXISTS (
    SELECT 1
    FROM sales_orders so
    JOIN customers c ON so.customer_id = c.customer_id
    WHERE so.sales_rep_id = e.employee_id
      AND so.order_status = 'cancelled'
      AND c.loyalty_tier = 'bronze'
)

========================================================================================================================
TEST 24 | employee_sets | hard | Employees above department benchmarks
========================================================================================================================
HTTP STATUS: 200
ENDPOINT SUCCESS: True
ELAPSED SECONDS: 98.41

NATURAL-LANGUAGE QUERIES
Q1: Which employees earn more than their department average and have a performance rating above 4?
Q2: Which employees earn more than the average salary in their department?
Q3: Which employees have a performance rating above 4?
Q4: Which employees earn below the company average and have a performance rating no higher than 3?

EXPECTED LOGICAL RELATIONSHIPS
- Q1 is contained in Q2.
- Q1 is contained in Q3.
- Q4 is not implied by the first three.

GENERATED SQL
Q2: success=True safe=True rows=21 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=97.0
SELECT e.employee_id, e.first_name, e.last_name, e.salary, e.performance_rating
FROM employees e
JOIN departments d ON e.department_id = d.department_id
WHERE e.salary > (
    SELECT AVG(e2.salary)
    FROM employees e2
    WHERE e2.department_id = e.department_id
)
AND e.performance_rating > 4
Q3: success=True safe=True rows=59 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=100.0
SELECT e.employee_id, e.first_name, e.last_name, e.salary, e.department_id
FROM employees e
WHERE e.salary > (
    SELECT AVG(e2.salary)
    FROM employees e2

========================================================================================================================
HTTP STATUS: 200
ENDPOINT SUCCESS: True
ELAPSED SECONDS: 78.14

NATURAL-LANGUAGE QUERIES
Q1: Which open temperature-controlled warehouses in the Northwest region hold low-stock Electronics products?
Q2: Which open temperature-controlled warehouses are in the Northwest region?
Q3: Which warehouses hold at least one low-stock Electronics product?
Q4: Which closed warehouses have no inventory records?

GENERATED SQL
Q2: success=True safe=True rows=0 source=llm_sql_repair score=100.0
SELECT w.warehouse_id, w.warehouse_name, w.warehouse_code
FROM warehouses w
JOIN inventory i ON w.warehouse_id = i.warehouse_id
JOIN products p ON i.product_id = p.product_id
WHERE w.region = 'Northwest'
  AND w.temperature_controlled = 1
  AND p.category = 'Electronics'
  AND i.quantity_on_hand < i.reorder_point
GROUP BY w.warehouse_id, w.warehouse_name, w.warehouse_code
HAVING SUM(i.quantity_on_hand) < SUM(i.reorder_point)
Q3: success=True safe=True rows=0 source=llm_sql_repair score=98.0

FROM warehouses
WHERE warehouses.region = 'Northwest'
  AND warehouses.temperature_controlled = 1
  AND warehouses.operating_status = 'active'
Q4: success=True safe=True rows=10 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=89.0

TEST 27 | warehouse_sets | hard | Warehouses serving Washington with risky stock
========================================================================================================================
HTTP STATUS: 200
ENDPOINT SUCCESS: True
ELAPSED SECONDS: 86.17

NATURAL-LANGUAGE QUERIES
Q1: Which warehouses delivered shipments to Washington and hold products from high-risk suppliers?
Q2: Which warehouses have delivered at least one shipment to Washington?
Q3: Which warehouses hold products from high-risk suppliers?
Q4: Which warehouses have inventory but have never originated a shipment?

EXPECTED LOGICAL RELATIONSHIPS
- Q1 is contained in Q2.
- Q1 is contained in Q3.
- Q4 is generally incomparable.

GENERATED SQL
Q2: success=True safe=True rows=12 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=99.0
SELECT w.warehouse_id, w.warehouse_name
FROM warehouses w
JOIN shipments s ON w.warehouse_id = s.warehouse_id
JOIN sales_orders so ON s.order_id = so.order_id
JOIN sales_order_items soi ON so.order_id = soi.order_id
JOIN products p ON soi.product_id = p.product_id
JOIN suppliers sup ON p.supplier_id = sup.supplier_id
JOIN customers c ON so.customer_id = c.customer_id
WHERE s.shipping_address_id IS NOT NULL
  AND EXISTS (
    SELECT 1
    FROM addresses a
    WHERE a.address_id = s.shipping_address_id
      AND a.state_code = 'WA'
  )
  AND sup.risk_level = 'high'
GROUP BY w.warehouse_id, w.warehouse_name
Q3: success=True safe=True rows=12 source=llm_sql_repair score=87.0
SELECT w.warehouse_id, w.warehouse_name
FROM warehouses w
JOIN shipments s ON w.warehouse_id = s.warehouse_id
JOIN addresses a ON s.shipping_address_id = a.address_id
WHERE a.state_code = 'WA'
GROUP BY w.warehouse_id, w.warehouse_name
HAVING COUNT(s.shipment_id) >= 1
Q4: success=True safe=True rows=12 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=96.0
SELECT DISTINCT w.warehouse_id, w.warehouse_name
FROM warehouses w
JOIN inventory i ON w.warehouse_id = i.warehouse_id
JOIN products p ON i.product_id = p.product_id
JOIN suppliers s ON p.supplier_id = s.supplier_id
WHERE s.risk_level = 'high'
GROUP BY w.warehouse_id, w.warehouse_name
Q5: success=True safe=True rows=0 source=llm_sql_repair score=87.0

FROM warehouses w

WHERE NOT EXISTS (
    SELECT 1
    FROM shipments s
    WHERE s.warehouse_id = w.warehouse_id
)
GROUP BY w.warehouse_id, w.warehouse_name

========================================================================================================================
TEST 28 | warehouse_sets | hard | Warehouses supporting multiple sales channels
========================================================================================================================
HTTP STATUS: 200
ENDPOINT SUCCESS: True
ELAPSED SECONDS: 95.99

NATURAL-LANGUAGE QUERIES
Q1: Which warehouses stocked products sold through both online and partner orders but never through store orders?
Q2: Which warehouses stocked products sold online?
Q3: Which warehouses stocked products sold through the partner channel?
Q4: Which warehouses stocked products sold through store orders but never online?

EXPECTED LOGICAL RELATIONSHIPS
- Q1 is contained in Q2.
- Q1 is contained in Q3.
- Q1 and Q4 should be disjoint.

GENERATED SQL
Q2: success=True safe=True rows=0 source=llm_sql_repair score=88.0
SELECT w.warehouse_id, w.warehouse_name
FROM warehouses w
WHERE EXISTS (
    SELECT 1
    FROM sales_order_items soi
    JOIN sales_orders so ON soi.order_id = so.order_id
    WHERE soi.warehouse_id = w.warehouse_id
    AND so.sales_channel = 'online'
)
AND EXISTS (
    SELECT 1
    FROM sales_order_items soi
    JOIN sales_orders so ON soi.order_id = so.order_id
    WHERE soi.warehouse_id = w.warehouse_id
    AND so.sales_channel = 'partner'
)
AND NOT EXISTS (
    SELECT 1
    FROM sales_order_items soi
    JOIN sales_orders so ON soi.order_id = so.order_id
    WHERE soi.warehouse_id = w.warehouse_id
    AND so.sales_channel = 'store'
)
WARNINGS: ['selected SQL: possible contradictory constraint']
Q3: success=True safe=True rows=12 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=99.0
SELECT w.warehouse_id, w.warehouse_name
FROM warehouses w
JOIN sales_order_items soi ON w.warehouse_id = soi.warehouse_id
JOIN sales_orders so ON soi.order_id = so.order_id
WHERE so.sales_channel = 'online'
GROUP BY w.warehouse_id, w.warehouse_name
Q4: success=True safe=True rows=12 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=95.0
SELECT w.warehouse_id, w.warehouse_name
FROM warehouses w
JOIN sales_order_items soi ON w.warehouse_id = soi.warehouse_id
JOIN sales_orders so ON soi.order_id = so.order_id
GROUP BY w.warehouse_id, w.warehouse_name
HAVING COUNT(CASE WHEN so.sales_channel = 'partner' THEN 1 END) > 0
Q5: success=True safe=True rows=0 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=97.0
SELECT w.warehouse_id, w.warehouse_name
FROM warehouses w
JOIN sales_order_items soi ON w.warehouse_id = soi.warehouse_id
JOIN sales_orders so ON soi.order_id = so.order_id
WHERE w.warehouse_id IN (
    SELECT DISTINCT soi2.warehouse_id
    FROM sales_order_items soi2
    JOIN sales_orders so2 ON soi2.order_id = so2.order_id
    WHERE so2.sales_channel = 'store'
)
AND w.warehouse_id NOT IN (
    SELECT DISTINCT soi3.warehouse_id
    FROM sales_order_items soi3
    JOIN sales_orders so3 ON soi3.order_id = so3.order_id
    WHERE so3.sales_channel = 'online'
)
GROUP BY w.warehouse_id, w.warehouse_name

Q1: Which warehouses have shipped more units than their current available inventory and are over 80 percent utilized?
Q2: Which warehouses have shipped more units than they currently have available?
Q3: Which warehouses are more than 80 percent utilized?
Q4: Which warehouses have never shipped an order item and are below 50 percent utilization?

- Q1 is contained in Q2.
- Q1 is contained in Q3.

GENERATED SQL
Q2: success=True safe=True rows=0 source=llm_sql_repair score=92.0
WITH shipped_per_warehouse AS (
    SELECT warehouse_id, SUM(quantity_shipped) AS total_shipped
    FROM sales_order_items
    GROUP BY warehouse_id
),
available_per_warehouse AS (
    SELECT warehouse_id, SUM(quantity_available) AS total_available
    FROM inventory
    GROUP BY warehouse_id
)
SELECT w.warehouse_id, w.warehouse_name
FROM warehouses w
JOIN shipped_per_warehouse sp ON w.warehouse_id = sp.warehouse_id
JOIN available_per_warehouse av ON w.warehouse_id = av.warehouse_id
WHERE w.current_utilization_pct > 80
  AND sp.total_shipped > av.total_available
Q3: success=True safe=True rows=0 source=llm_sql_repair score=87.0

TEST 30 | warehouse_sets | hard | Regions handling selected categories
========================================================================================================================
HTTP STATUS: 200
ENDPOINT SUCCESS: True
ELAPSED SECONDS: 109.49

NATURAL-LANGUAGE QUERIES
Q1: Which warehouse regions handled both Electronics and Apparel items but no Automotive items?
Q2: Which warehouse regions handled Electronics items?
Q3: Which warehouse regions handled Apparel items?
Q4: Which warehouse regions handled Automotive items but no Electronics items?

EXPECTED LOGICAL RELATIONSHIPS
- Q1 is contained in Q2.
- Q1 is contained in Q3.
- Q1 and Q4 should be disjoint.

GENERATED SQL
Q2: success=True safe=True rows=0 source=llm_sql_repair score=88.0
SELECT w.warehouse_id, w.region
FROM warehouses w
JOIN sales_order_items soi ON w.warehouse_id = soi.warehouse_id
JOIN products p ON soi.product_id = p.product_id
GROUP BY w.warehouse_id, w.region
HAVING COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN p.category = 'Electronics' THEN soi.order_item_id END) >= 1
   AND COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN p.category = 'Apparel' THEN soi.order_item_id END) >= 1
   AND COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN p.category = 'Automotive' THEN soi.order_item_id END) = 0
WARNINGS: ['selected SQL: possible contradictory constraint']
Q3: success=True safe=True rows=7 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=100.0
SELECT w.region
FROM warehouses w
JOIN inventory i ON w.warehouse_id = i.warehouse_id
JOIN products p ON i.product_id = p.product_id
WHERE p.category = 'Electronics'
GROUP BY w.region
HAVING COUNT(DISTINCT i.inventory_id) > 0
Q4: success=True safe=True rows=7 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=90.0

Q5: success=True safe=True rows=0 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=88.0
SELECT w.warehouse_id, w.region
FROM warehouses w
JOIN sales_order_items soi ON w.warehouse_id = soi.warehouse_id
JOIN products p ON soi.product_id = p.product_id
WHERE p.category = 'Automotive'
AND NOT EXISTS (
    SELECT 1
    FROM sales_order_items soi2
    JOIN products p2 ON soi2.product_id = p2.product_id
    WHERE soi2.warehouse_id = w.warehouse_id

)

TEST 32 | shipment_sets | moderate | FedEx overnight deliveries to Washington
========================================================================================================================
HTTP STATUS: 200
ENDPOINT SUCCESS: True
ELAPSED SECONDS: 96.39

NATURAL-LANGUAGE QUERIES
Q1: Which FedEx shipments used overnight service and went to Washington?
Q2: Which FedEx shipments went to Washington?
Q3: Which overnight shipments went to Washington?
Q4: Which UPS freight shipments went to Idaho?

EXPECTED LOGICAL RELATIONSHIPS
- Q1 is contained in Q2.
- Q1 is contained in Q3.
- Q4 is a different shipment set.

GENERATED SQL
Q2: success=True safe=True rows=5 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=100.0
SELECT s.shipment_id, s.shipment_number, s.carrier, s.service_level, a.city, a.state_code
FROM shipments s
JOIN addresses a ON s.shipping_address_id = a.address_id
WHERE s.carrier = 'FedEx'
  AND s.service_level = 'overnight'
  AND a.state_code = 'WA'
Q3: success=True safe=True rows=28 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=95.0
SELECT s.shipment_id, s.shipment_number, s.carrier, s.tracking_number, s.ship_date, s.actual_delivery_date
FROM shipments s
JOIN addresses a ON s.shipping_address_id = a.address_id
WHERE s.carrier = 'FedEx'
  AND a.state_code = 'WA'
Q4: success=True safe=True rows=33 source=llm_sql_repair score=94.0
SELECT s.shipment_id, s.shipment_number, s.carrier, s.service_level, s.tracking_number, s.ship_date, s.actual_delivery_date, a.city
FROM shipments s
JOIN addresses a ON s.shipping_address_id = a.address_id
WHERE s.service_level = 'overnight' AND a.state_code = 'WA'
Q5: success=True safe=True rows=11 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=97.0

Q1: Which shipments belong to online orders from Gold customers that contained Electronics products?

Q4: Which shipments belong to store orders from Bronze customers with no Electronics items?

- Q4 is a different shipment set.

GENERATED SQL
Q2: success=True safe=True rows=24 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=100.0
SELECT s.shipment_id, s.shipment_number, s.order_id, c.loyalty_tier, p.category
FROM shipments s
JOIN sales_orders so ON s.order_id = so.order_id
JOIN customers c ON so.customer_id = c.customer_id
JOIN sales_order_items soi ON so.order_id = soi.order_id
JOIN products p ON soi.product_id = p.product_id
WHERE c.loyalty_tier = 'gold'
  AND so.sales_channel = 'online'
  AND p.category = 'Electronics'
Q3: success=True safe=True rows=46 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=100.0

FROM shipments s
JOIN sales_orders so ON s.order_id = so.order_id
JOIN customers c ON so.customer_id = c.customer_id
WHERE c.loyalty_tier = 'gold'
  AND so.sales_channel = 'online'
Q4: success=True safe=True rows=344 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=91.0
SELECT DISTINCT s.shipment_id, s.shipment_number, s.order_id
FROM shipments s
JOIN sales_orders so ON s.order_id = so.order_id
JOIN sales_order_items soi ON so.order_id = soi.order_id
JOIN products p ON soi.product_id = p.product_id
WHERE p.category = 'Electronics'
Q5: success=True safe=True rows=0 source=llm_sql_repair score=90.0
SELECT s.shipment_id, s.shipment_number, s.order_id
FROM shipments s
JOIN sales_orders so ON s.order_id = so.order_id
JOIN customers c ON so.customer_id = c.customer_id
WHERE c.loyalty_tier = 'Bronze'
AND NOT EXISTS (
    SELECT 1
    FROM sales_order_items soi
    JOIN products p ON soi.product_id = p.product_id
    WHERE soi.order_id = so.order_id
    AND p.category = 'Electronics'
)

GENERATED SQL
Q2: success=True safe=True rows=177 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=100.0
SELECT s.shipment_id, s.carrier, s.shipping_cost, s.total_weight_kg
FROM shipments s
WHERE s.shipping_cost > (
    SELECT AVG(s2.shipping_cost)
    FROM shipments s2
    WHERE s2.carrier = s.carrier
)
AND s.total_weight_kg > (
    SELECT AVG(s3.total_weight_kg)
    FROM shipments s3
    WHERE s3.carrier = s.carrier
)

HTTP STATUS: 200
ENDPOINT SUCCESS: True
ELAPSED SECONDS: 94.51

NATURAL-LANGUAGE QUERIES
Q1: Which settled credit-card payments came from enterprise customers during 2025?
Q2: Which settled payments came from enterprise customers during 2025?
Q3: Which credit-card payments came from enterprise customers during 2025?
Q4: Which failed ACH payments came from individual customers?

EXPECTED LOGICAL RELATIONSHIPS
- Q1 is contained in Q2.
- Q1 is contained in Q3.
- Q4 is a different payment set.

GENERATED SQL
Q2: success=True safe=True rows=0 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=94.0
SELECT p.payment_id, p.payment_number, p.amount, c.customer_id, c.customer_segment
FROM payments p
JOIN customers c ON p.customer_id = c.customer_id
WHERE p.payment_status = 'settled'
  AND p.payment_method = 'credit-card'
  AND c.customer_segment = 'enterprise'
  AND p.payment_date LIKE '2025%'
WARNINGS: ["selected SQL uses literal 'credit-card' not found in sampled values of 'payment_method' (known: ['ach', 'check', 'credit_card', 'paypal', 'wire'])"]
Q3: success=True safe=True rows=29 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=100.0
SELECT p.payment_id, p.payment_number, p.payment_date, p.amount, c.customer_id, c.customer_segment
FROM payments p
JOIN customers c ON p.customer_id = c.customer_id
WHERE p.payment_status = 'settled'
  AND c.customer_segment = 'enterprise'
  AND p.payment_date LIKE '2025%'
Q4: success=True safe=True rows=13 source=llm_primary score=100.0
SELECT "payments"."payment_id", "payments"."payment_number", "payments"."payment_date", "payments"."amount" FROM "payments" INNER JOIN "customers" ON "payments"."customer_id" = "customers"."customer_id" WHERE "payments"."payment_method" = ? AND "customers"."customer_segment" = ? AND "payments"."payment_date" >= ? AND "payments"."payment_date" < ?
Q5: success=True safe=True rows=0 source=llm_sql_repair score=100.0
SELECT p.payment_id, p.payment_number, p.amount, c.customer_id, c.customer_segment
FROM payments p
JOIN customers c ON p.customer_id = c.customer_id
WHERE p.payment_status = 'failed'
  AND p.payment_method = 'ACH'
  AND c.customer_segment = 'retail'

GENERATED SQL
Q2: success=True safe=True rows=75 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=100.0
SELECT p.payment_id, p.payment_number, p.amount, p.payment_method, c.loyalty_tier
FROM payments p
JOIN customers c ON p.customer_id = c.customer_id
WHERE c.loyalty_tier = 'gold'
  AND p.amount > (
    SELECT AVG(p2.amount)
    FROM payments p2
    WHERE p2.payment_method = p.payment_method
  )
Q3: success=True safe=True rows=360 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=100.0

    FROM payments p2
    WHERE p2.payment_method = p.payment_method
)

Q5: success=True safe=True rows=154 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=100.0

NATURAL-LANGUAGE QUERIES
Q1: Which customer segments generated more than 50,000 dollars in delivered-order revenue and kept their refund rate below 5 percent?
Q2: Which customer segments generated more than 50,000 dollars in delivered-order revenue?
Q3: Which customer segments have a refund rate below 5 percent?
Q4: Which customer segments generated no delivered-order revenue?

EXPECTED LOGICAL RELATIONSHIPS
- Q1 is contained in Q2.
- Q1 is contained in Q3.

GENERATED SQL
Q2: success=True safe=True rows=4 source=llm_sql_repair score=88.0
WITH order_totals AS (
    SELECT 
        c.customer_segment,
        SUM(so.grand_total) AS total_revenue
    FROM customers c
    JOIN sales_orders so ON c.customer_id = so.customer_id
    WHERE so.order_status = 'delivered'
    GROUP BY c.customer_segment
),
refund_totals AS (
    SELECT 
        c.customer_segment,
        SUM(p.refunded_amount) AS total_refunded
    FROM customers c
    JOIN payments p ON c.customer_id = p.customer_id
    JOIN sales_orders so ON p.order_id = so.order_id
    WHERE so.order_status = 'delivered'
    GROUP BY c.customer_segment
)
SELECT 
    ot.customer_segment
FROM order_totals ot
JOIN refund_totals rt ON ot.customer_segment = rt.customer_segment
WHERE ot.total_revenue > 50000
  AND rt.total_refunded < ot.total_revenue * 0.05
WARNINGS: ['selected SQL: possible join fanout aggregate inflation']

========================================================================================================================
TEST 42 | aggregate_sets | hard | Categories with margin and channel reach
========================================================================================================================
HTTP STATUS: 200
ENDPOINT SUCCESS: True
ELAPSED SECONDS: 90.86

NATURAL-LANGUAGE QUERIES
Q1: Which product categories have gross margin above 40 percent and were sold through both online and partner orders?
Q2: Which product categories have gross margin above 40 percent?
Q3: Which product categories were sold through both online and partner orders?
Q4: Which product categories have never been sold online?

EXPECTED LOGICAL RELATIONSHIPS
- Q1 is contained in Q2.
- Q1 is contained in Q3.
- Q4 should not contain Q1.

GENERATED SQL
Q2: success=True safe=True rows=7 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=90.0
SELECT p.category
FROM products p
JOIN sales_order_items soi ON p.product_id = soi.product_id
JOIN sales_orders so ON soi.order_id = so.order_id
GROUP BY p.category
HAVING 
  SUM(soi.quantity_ordered * (soi.unit_price - soi.unit_cost)) * 100.0 / NULLIF(SUM(soi.quantity_ordered * soi.unit_price), 0) > 40
  AND COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN so.sales_channel = 'online' THEN 1 END) > 0
  AND COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN so.sales_channel = 'partner' THEN 1 END) > 0
WARNINGS: ['selected SQL: possible join fanout aggregate inflation']
Q3: success=True safe=True rows=7 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=100.0
SELECT p.category
FROM products p
JOIN sales_order_items soi ON p.product_id = soi.product_id
GROUP BY p.category
HAVING (AVG(soi.unit_price) - AVG(soi.unit_cost)) * 100.0 / AVG(soi.unit_price) > 40
Q4: success=True safe=True rows=8 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=100.0
SELECT p.category
FROM products p
JOIN sales_order_items soi ON p.product_id = soi.product_id
JOIN sales_orders so ON soi.order_id = so.order_id
GROUP BY p.category
HAVING COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN so.sales_channel = 'online' THEN so.sales_channel END) > 0
   AND COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN so.sales_channel = 'partner' THEN so.sales_channel END) > 0
Q5: success=True safe=True rows=8 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=100.0
SELECT p.category
FROM products p
WHERE NOT EXISTS (
    SELECT 1
    FROM sales_order_items soi
    JOIN sales_orders so ON soi.order_id = so.order_id
    WHERE soi.product_id = p.product_id
      AND so.sales_channel = 'online'
)
GROUP BY p.category

TEST 44 | aggregate_sets | hard | Efficient carriers
========================================================================================================================
HTTP STATUS: 200
ENDPOINT SUCCESS: True

NATURAL-LANGUAGE QUERIES
Q1: Which carriers have an on-time delivery rate above 90 percent and average shipping cost below the overall average?
Q2: Which carriers have an on-time delivery rate above 90 percent?

- Q1 is contained in Q2.
- Q1 is contained in Q3.

GENERATED SQL
Q2: success=True safe=True rows=0 source=llm_sql_direct score=100.0
SELECT carrier
FROM shipments
WHERE shipment_status = 'delivered'
GROUP BY carrier
HAVING (SUM(CASE WHEN actual_delivery_date <= estimated_delivery_date THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) * 100.0 / COUNT(*)) > 90
   AND AVG(shipping_cost) < (SELECT AVG(shipping_cost) FROM shipments)
Q3: success=True safe=True rows=0 source=llm_sql_repair score=88.0

FROM shipments

HAVING (CAST(SUM(CASE WHEN shipments.shipment_status = 'delivered' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS REAL) * 100.0 / COUNT(shipments.shipment_id)) > 90

TEST 45 | aggregate_sets | hard | Suppliers with revenue and broad stocking
========================================================================================================================
HTTP STATUS: 200
ENDPOINT SUCCESS: True
ELAPSED SECONDS: 87.07

NATURAL-LANGUAGE QUERIES
Q1: Which suppliers generated more than 20,000 dollars in delivered-order revenue and have products stored in at least three warehouses?
Q2: Which suppliers generated more than 20,000 dollars in delivered-order revenue?
Q3: Which suppliers have products stored in at least three warehouses?
Q4: Which suppliers have products that have never appeared on an order?

EXPECTED LOGICAL RELATIONSHIPS
- Q1 is contained in Q2.
- Q1 is contained in Q3.
- Q4 is generally incomparable.

GENERATED SQL
Q2: success=True safe=True rows=60 source=llm_sql_repair score=89.0
WITH supplier_revenue AS (
    SELECT
        p.supplier_id,
        SUM(soi.line_total) AS total_revenue
    FROM products p
    JOIN sales_order_items soi ON p.product_id = soi.product_id
    JOIN sales_orders so ON soi.order_id = so.order_id
    WHERE so.order_status = 'delivered'
    GROUP BY p.supplier_id
),
supplier_warehouse_count AS (
    SELECT
        p.supplier_id,
        COUNT(DISTINCT i.warehouse_id) AS warehouse_count
    FROM products p
    JOIN inventory i ON p.product_id = i.product_id
    GROUP BY p.supplier_id
)
SELECT
    s.supplier_id,
    s.supplier_name
FROM suppliers s
JOIN supplier_revenue sr ON s.supplier_id = sr.supplier_id
JOIN supplier_warehouse_count swc ON s.supplier_id = swc.supplier_id
WHERE sr.total_revenue > 20000
  AND swc.warehouse_count >= 3
WARNINGS: ['selected SQL: possible join fanout aggregate inflation']

========================================================================================================================
TEST 46 | set_subquery_sets | hard | Customers active across years
========================================================================================================================
HTTP STATUS: 200
ENDPOINT SUCCESS: True
ELAPSED SECONDS: 113.40

NATURAL-LANGUAGE QUERIES
Q1: Which customers had delivered orders in both 2024 and 2025 but none in 2026?
Q2: Which customers had delivered orders in both 2024 and 2025?
Q3: Which customers had no delivered orders in 2026?
Q4: Which customers had delivered orders only in 2026?

EXPECTED LOGICAL RELATIONSHIPS
- Q1 is contained in Q2.
- Q1 is contained in Q3.
- Q1 and Q4 should be disjoint.

GENERATED SQL
Q2: success=True safe=True rows=68 source=llm_sql_direct_grain score=90.0
SELECT c.customer_id, c.first_name, c.last_name
FROM customers c
JOIN sales_orders so ON c.customer_id = so.customer_id
WHERE so.order_status = 'delivered'
  AND strftime('%Y', so.shipped_date) IN ('2024', '2025')
GROUP BY c.customer_id, c.first_name, c.last_name
HAVING COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN strftime('%Y', so.shipped_date) = '2024' THEN so.order_id END) > 0
   AND COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN strftime('%Y', so.shipped_date) = '2025' THEN so.order_id END) > 0
   AND COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN strftime('%Y', so.shipped_date) = '2026' THEN so.order_id END) = 0
Q3: success=True safe=True rows=68 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=100.0
SELECT c.customer_id, c.full_name
FROM customers c
JOIN sales_orders so ON c.customer_id = so.customer_id
WHERE so.order_status = 'delivered'
  AND so.shipped_date IS NOT NULL
  AND (strftime('%Y', so.shipped_date) = '2024' OR strftime('%Y', so.shipped_date) = '2025')
GROUP BY c.customer_id, c.full_name
HAVING COUNT(DISTINCT strftime('%Y', so.shipped_date)) = 2
Q4: success=True safe=True rows=199 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=99.0
SELECT c.customer_id, c.first_name, c.last_name
FROM customers c
WHERE NOT EXISTS (
    SELECT 1
    FROM sales_orders so
    JOIN shipments s ON s.order_id = so.order_id
    WHERE so.customer_id = c.customer_id
      AND so.order_date LIKE '2026%'
      AND s.shipment_status = 'delivered'
)
Q5: success=True safe=True rows=22 source=llm_sql_repair score=100.0
SELECT c.customer_id, c.first_name, c.last_name
FROM customers c
JOIN sales_orders so ON c.customer_id = so.customer_id
WHERE so.fulfillment_status = 'fulfilled'
  AND strftime('%Y', so.order_date) = '2026'
GROUP BY c.customer_id, c.first_name, c.last_name
HAVING COUNT(*) = (
    SELECT COUNT(*)
    FROM sales_orders so2
    WHERE so2.customer_id = c.customer_id
      AND so2.fulfillment_status = 'fulfilled'
)

CONTAINMENT SUMMARY
None: status=incomparable_with_all_tested | contained_in=- | contains=- | equivalent_to=- | incomparable_with=[3, 4] | unknown_with=[2]

None: status=incomparable_with_all_tested | contained_in=- | contains=- | equivalent_to=- | incomparable_with=[1, 2, 4] | unknown_with=-
None: status=incomparable_with_all_tested | contained_in=- | contains=- | equivalent_to=- | incomparable_with=[1, 3] | unknown_with=[2]

PAIRWISE RESULTS
None vs None: unknown
  Cannot compare grouped queries: different group keys (['customer_id', 'first_name', 'last_name'] vs ['customer_id', 'full_name']).

========================================================================================================================
TEST 47 | set_subquery_sets | hard | Products stocked everywhere and sold online
========================================================================================================================
HTTP STATUS: 200
ENDPOINT SUCCESS: True
ELAPSED SECONDS: 86.42

NATURAL-LANGUAGE QUERIES
Q1: Which products are stocked in every open warehouse and have been sold online?
Q2: Which products are stocked in every open warehouse?
Q3: Which products have been sold through the online channel?
Q4: Which products have no inventory records?

EXPECTED LOGICAL RELATIONSHIPS
- Q1 is contained in Q2.
- Q1 is contained in Q3.
- Q4 should be disjoint from Q1 and Q2.

GENERATED SQL
Q2: success=True safe=True rows=0 source=llm_sql_repair score=94.0
SELECT p.product_id, p.product_name
FROM products p
JOIN sales_order_items soi ON p.product_id = soi.product_id
JOIN sales_orders so ON soi.order_id = so.order_id
JOIN inventory i ON p.product_id = i.product_id
JOIN warehouses w ON i.warehouse_id = w.warehouse_id
WHERE so.sales_channel = 'online'
  AND w.operating_status = 'active'
GROUP BY p.product_id, p.product_name
HAVING COUNT(DISTINCT i.warehouse_id) = (
    SELECT COUNT(*)
    FROM warehouses
    WHERE operating_status = 'active'
)
Q3: success=True safe=True rows=0 source=llm_sql_repair score=93.0
SELECT p.product_id, p.product_name
FROM products p
JOIN inventory i ON p.product_id = i.product_id
JOIN warehouses w ON i.warehouse_id = w.warehouse_id
WHERE w.operating_status = 'active'
GROUP BY p.product_id, p.product_name

========================================================================================================================
TEST 50 | set_subquery_sets | hard | Customers with recent success and high lifetime value
========================================================================================================================
HTTP STATUS: 200
ENDPOINT SUCCESS: True
ELAPSED SECONDS: 79.07

NATURAL-LANGUAGE QUERIES
Q1: Which customers have a delivered most-recent order and total order value above the average customer total?
Q2: Which customers have a delivered order as their most recent order?
Q3: Which customers have total order value above the average customer total order value?
Q4: Which customers have never placed an order?

EXPECTED LOGICAL RELATIONSHIPS
- Q1 is contained in Q2.
- Q1 is contained in Q3.
- Q4 should be disjoint from Q1, Q2, and Q3.

GENERATED SQL
Q2: success=True safe=True rows=86 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=100.0
SELECT c.customer_id, c.full_name, c.customer_number
FROM customers c
JOIN sales_orders so ON c.customer_id = so.customer_id
GROUP BY c.customer_id, c.full_name, c.customer_number
HAVING SUM(so.grand_total) > (
    SELECT AVG(total_customer_value)
    FROM (
        SELECT SUM(grand_total) AS total_customer_value
        FROM sales_orders
        GROUP BY customer_id
    )
)
AND MAX(CASE WHEN so.order_status = 'delivered' THEN so.order_date END) = MAX(so.order_date)
Q3: success=True safe=True rows=187 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=100.0
WITH ranked_orders AS (
    SELECT 
        so.customer_id,
        so.order_status,
        so.order_date,
        ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY so.customer_id ORDER BY so.order_date DESC) AS rn
    FROM sales_orders so
    JOIN customers c ON so.customer_id = c.customer_id
)
SELECT 
    c.customer_id,
    c.first_name,
    c.last_name
FROM customers c
JOIN ranked_orders ro ON c.customer_id = ro.customer_id
WHERE ro.rn = 1 AND ro.order_status = 'delivered'
Q4: success=True safe=True rows=125 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=100.0
SELECT c.customer_id, c.full_name
FROM customers c
JOIN sales_orders o ON c.customer_id = o.customer_id
GROUP BY c.customer_id, c.full_name
HAVING SUM(o.grand_total) > (
    SELECT AVG(customer_total)
    FROM (
        SELECT SUM(grand_total) AS customer_total
        FROM sales_orders
        GROUP BY customer_id
    )
)
Q5: success=True safe=True rows=22 source=llm_sql_direct_variant score=99.0
SELECT c.customer_id, c.first_name, c.last_name
FROM customers c
WHERE NOT EXISTS (
    SELECT 1
    FROM sales_orders so
    WHERE so.customer_id = c.customer_id
)
